import * as React from "react";
import {
  DiagramCanvas,
  DiagramGrid,
  DiagramNode,
  DiagramConnection,
  DiagramMarker,
  DiagramCaption,
  ArrowheadDef,
} from "@/components/diagram";

// 1. Overall System Topology
export function OverallSystemDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 220;
  const patternId = "grid-system-overall";
  const nodeY = 80;
  const connectionY = 110;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 60;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Overall System Topology"
      description="Three-node system architecture: Website Portal entry point, Scheduler Core control plane, and Node Network execution plane. Connections show data flow from website to scheduler to compute nodes."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Website */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[WEBSITE_PORTAL]"
        detail="Entry & Onboard"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Control Plane"
      >
        <DiagramMarker cx={125} cy={15} />
      </DiagramNode>

      {/* Node 3: Contributed Nodes */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[NODE_NETWORK]"
        detail="Execution Plane"
      />

      {/* Connections */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth - 45} cy={connectionY} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 2. Request Flow
export function RequestFlowDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 240;
  const patternId = "grid-flow-request";
  const nodeY = 90;
  const connectionY = 120;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Request Flow"
      description="Request lifecycle from client submission through scheduler routing to node execution. Active path highlighted showing successful routing to EU-West node with direct result return path."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Client */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[CLIENT_INTERFACE]"
        detail="Status: SUBMITTING"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Status: ROUTING"
      />

      {/* Node 3: Selected Compute Node */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[NODE_EU_WEST]"
        detail="Status: EXECUTING"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Active Connection Paths */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      {/* Signal indicators on the active loop */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeWidth + 45} cy={connectionY} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 - 45} cy={connectionY} />

      {/* Direct Output Return Path (Subtle feedback loop at bottom) */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 + nodeWidth - 30}
        y1={connectionY + 30}
        x2={startX + 30}
        y2={connectionY + 30}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: width / 2, y: connectionY + 70 }}
      />
      <DiagramCaption
        x={width / 2}
        y={connectionY + 65}
        text="DIRECT_RESULT_PAYLOAD (verification_loop)"
      />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 3. Geographic Scheduling
export function GeographicSchedulingDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 280;
  const patternId = "grid-geo-scheduling";
  const schedulerX = 80;
  const schedulerY = 110;
  const nodeX = 480;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 50;
  const nodeSpacing = 75;
  const startY = 40;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Geographic Scheduling"
      description="Scheduler routing decision showing three candidate nodes with latency measurements. EU-West selected as minimum latency (12ms) vs US-East (78ms) and AP-South (284ms)."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Scheduler Node (Left Column) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={schedulerX}
        y={schedulerY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Latency Engine"
      />

      {/* Nodes (Right Column Stacked) */}
      {/* Node 1: US-East */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_US_EAST]"
        detail="Latency: 78ms"
      />

      {/* Node 2: EU-West (Selected) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY + nodeSpacing}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_EU_WEST]"
        detail="Latency: 12ms (MIN)"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Node 3: AP-South */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY + nodeSpacing * 2}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_AP_SOUTH]"
        detail="Latency: 284ms"
      />

      {/* Routing branches */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeHeight / 2}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: 350, y: 65 }}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeSpacing + nodeHeight / 2}
        active
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeSpacing * 2 + nodeHeight / 2}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: 350, y: 215 }}
      />

      <DiagramMarker cx={350} cy={schedulerY + 30} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 4. Distributed Inference
export function DistributedInferenceDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 280;
  const patternId = "grid-inf-distributed";
  const schedulerX = 80;
  const schedulerY = 110;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 50;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Distributed Inference Pipeline"
      description="Model layer partitioning across three compute shards. Scheduler partitions layers 1-12 to Shard A, 13-24 to Shard B, 25-36 to Shard C. Pipeline flow shown with active connections."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Scheduler (Left) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={schedulerX}
        y={schedulerY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Layer Partitioner"
      />

      {/* Pipeline Shards */}
      {/* Shard A */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={320}
        y={60}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_A]"
        detail="Layers: 1 - 12"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Shard B */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={520}
        y={60}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_B]"
        detail="Layers: 13 - 24"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Shard C */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={420}
        y={170}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_C]"
        detail="Layers: 25 - 36"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Pipeline connection paths */}
      {/* Scheduler -> Shard A */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={320}
        y2={85}
        active
      />

      {/* Shard A -> Shard B */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={460}
        y1={85}
        x2={520}
        y2={85}
        active
      />

      {/* Shard B -> Shard C */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={590}
        y1={110}
        x2={490}
        y2={170}
        active
      />

      {/* Flow ticks along the pipeline */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={270} cy={112.5} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={490} cy={85} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={540} cy={140} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 5. Future Architecture
export function PlatformStackDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 240;
  const patternId = "grid-stack-platform";
  const layerX = 120;
  const layerWidth = 520;
  const layerHeight = 35;
  const layerSpacing = 45;
  const startY = 30;

  const layers = [
    {
      label: "APPLICATION / API LAYER",
      detail: "Client SDKs, telemetry portals, developer API endpoints",
      y: startY,
      active: false,
    },
    {
      label: "ORCHESTRATION & COORDINATION LAYER",
      detail: "Geographic scheduling engine, node registries, queue models",
      y: startY + layerSpacing,
      active: true,
    },
    {
      label: "DECENTRALIZED TRANSPORT LAYER",
      detail: "P2P overlay routing, message heartbeats, secure gRPC tunnels",
      y: startY + layerSpacing * 2,
      active: false,
    },
    {
      label: "LOCAL HARDWARE EXECUTION RUNTIME",
      detail: "CUDA/ROCm device engines, local resource benchmarks, sandboxes",
      y: startY + layerSpacing * 3,
      active: false,
    },
  ];

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Future Platform Stack Architecture"
      description="Four-layer platform stack: Application API layer, Orchestration & Coordination layer (active), Decentralized Transport layer, and Local Hardware Execution Runtime layer. Each layer spans full width with descriptive details."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {layers.map((layer, index) => (
        <DiagramNode
          key={index}
          x={layerX}
          y={layer.y}
          width={layerWidth}
          height={layerHeight}
          label={layer.label}
          detail={layer.detail}
          active={layer.active}
          detailActive={layer.active}
        />
      ))}
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

import * as React from "react";
import {
  DiagramCanvas,
  DiagramGrid,
  DiagramNode,
  DiagramConnection,
  DiagramMarker,
  ArrowheadDef,
} from "@/components/diagram";

export function SystemDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 180;
  const patternId = "grid-home-system";
  const nodeY = 60;
  const connectionY = 90;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 60;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Public Intelligence System Overview"
      description="Three core components: Website Portal for onboarding, Scheduler Core as coordinator, and Compute Network for execution. Active connection from scheduler to compute network indicated by lime markers."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Website */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[WEBSITE_PORTAL]"
        detail="Role: Onboarding"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Role: Coordinator"
      >
        <DiagramMarker cx={125} cy={15} />
      </DiagramNode>

      {/* Node 3: Global Compute Network */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[COMPUTE_NETWORK]"
        detail="Role: Execution"
      />

      {/* CONNECTIONS (Aligned at Y=90) */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      {/* Data indicator dot */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 - 45} cy={connectionY} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

              Geographic Scheduling
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">

          </header>
          <GeographicSchedulingDiagram />
        </section>

        <section className="space-y-16">
          <header className="space-y-4">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-foreground">
              Distributed Inference
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">
              Model layer partitioning across multiple compute shards for large-scale inference.
              Each shard processes a contiguous layer range with pipelined tensor passing.
            </p>
          </header>
          <DistributedInferenceDiagram />
        </section>

        <section className="space-y-16">

              Future Platform Stack
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">
              Four-layer architecture vision: application APIs, orchestration coordination,
              decentralized transport, and local hardware runtime. The coordination layer is the
              active development focus.
            </p>
          </header>
          <PlatformStackDiagram />
        </section>
      </article>
    </PageShell>
  );
}

src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramCanvasProps = {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  className?: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
};

export function DiagramCanvas({
  children,
  width = 760,
  height = 240,
  className = "",
  title,
  description,
}: DiagramCanvasProps) {
  const titleId = `diagram-title-${React.useId()}`;
  const descId = `diagram-desc-${React.useId()}`;

  return (
    <div className={`w-full flex justify-center py-4 ${className}`}>
      <svg
        viewBox={`0 0 ${width} ${height}`}
        fill="none"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        className="w-full max-w-4xl font-mono"
        role="img"
        aria-labelledby={titleId}
        aria-describedby={descId}
      >
        <title id={titleId}>{title}</title>
        <desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>
        <defs>
          <pattern
            id={`grid-${React.useId()}`}
            width="20"
            height="20"
            patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse"
          >
            <path
              d="M 20 0 L 0 0 0 20"
              fill="none"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="0.5"
              strokeOpacity="0.03"
            />
          </pattern>
        </defs>
        <rect
          width={width}
          height={height}
          fill={`url(#grid-${React.useId()})`}
          rx="6"
        />
        {children}
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}
```

src/components/diagram/DiagramGrid.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramGridProps = {
  width: number;
  height: number;
  patternId: string;
};

export function DiagramGrid({ width, height, patternId }: DiagramGridProps) {
  return (
    <>
      <rect width={width} height={height} fill={`url(#${patternId})`} rx="6" />
      <rect
        x="0.5"
        y="0.5"
        width={width - 1}
        height={height - 1}
        rx="6"
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="1"
        strokeOpacity="0.08"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d="M 10 0.5 L 0.5 0.5 L 0.5 10"
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="1"
        strokeOpacity="0.25"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${width - 10} 0.5 L ${width - 0.5} 0.5 L ${width - 0.5} 10`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="1"
        strokeOpacity="0.25"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M 0.5 ${height - 10} L 0.5 ${height - 0.5} L 10 ${height - 0.5}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="1"
        strokeOpacity="0.25"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${width - 10} ${height - 0.5} L ${width - 0.5} ${height - 0.5} L ${width - 0.5} ${height - 10}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="1"
        strokeOpacity="0.25"
        fill="none"
      />
    </>
  );
}
```

src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramNodeProps = {
  x: number;
  y: number;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  label: string;
  detail: string;
  active?: boolean;
  detailActive?: boolean;
  children?: React.ReactNode;
};

const NODE_WIDTH = 140;
const NODE_HEIGHT = 60;
const NODE_HEIGHT_COMPACT = 50;
const BORDER_RADIUS = 3;
const STROKE_WIDTH = 1;

export function DiagramNode({
  x,
  y,
  width = NODE_WIDTH,
  height = NODE_HEIGHT,
  label,
  detail,
  active = false,
  detailActive = false,
  children,
}: DiagramNodeProps) {
  return (
    <g transform={`translate(${x}, ${y})`}>
      <rect
        x="0"
        y="0"
        width={width}
        height={height}
        rx={BORDER_RADIUS}
        stroke={active ? "#D9F99D" : "currentColor"}
        strokeWidth={STROKE_WIDTH}
        strokeOpacity={active ? 0.4 : 0.18}
        fill="var(--background, #0f0f11)"
      />
      <text
        x="15"
        y={height === NODE_HEIGHT_COMPACT ? 20 : 24}
        fill={active ? "#D9F99D" : "#f3f4f6"}
        fontSize="11"
        fontWeight="600"
      >
        {label}
      </text>
      <text
        x="15"
        y={height === NODE_HEIGHT_COMPACT ? 36 : 42}
        fill={detailActive ? "#d1d5db" : active ? "#d1d5db" : "#9ca3af"}
        fontSize="9.5"
        fontWeight={detailActive ? "500" : "400"}
      >
        {detail}
      </text>
      {children}
    </g>
  );
}
```

src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramConnectionProps = {
  x1: number;
  y1: number;
  x2: number;
  y2: number;
  active?: boolean;
  curved?: boolean;
  controlPoint?: { x: number; y: number };
  marker?: boolean;
};

export function DiagramConnection({
  x1,
  y1,
  x2,
  y2,
  active = false,
  curved = false,
  controlPoint,
  marker = false,
}: DiagramConnectionProps) {
  const stroke = active ? "#D9F99D" : "currentColor";
  const strokeWidth = active ? 1.2 : 1;
  const strokeOpacity = active ? 1 : 0.1;
  const strokeDasharray = active ? "none" : "3 3";

  if (curved && controlPoint) {
    return (
      <path
        d={`M ${x1} ${y1} Q ${controlPoint.x} ${controlPoint.y} ${x2} ${y2}`}
        stroke={stroke}
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
        strokeOpacity={strokeOpacity}
        strokeDasharray={strokeDasharray}
        fill="none"
        markerEnd={marker ? "url(#arrowhead)" : undefined}
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <line
      x1={x1}
      y1={y1}
      x2={x2}
      y2={y2}
      stroke={stroke}
      strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
      strokeOpacity={strokeOpacity}
      strokeDasharray={strokeDasharray}
      markerEnd={marker ? "url(#arrowhead)" : undefined}
    />
  );
}
```

src/components/diagram/DiagramMarker.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramMarkerProps = {
  cx: number;
  cy: number;
  r?: number;
  fill?: string;
};

export function DiagramMarker({ cx, cy, r = 2.5, fill = "#D9F99D" }: DiagramMarkerProps) {
  return <circle cx={cx} cy={cy} r={r} fill={fill} />;
}
```

src/components/diagram/DiagramCaption.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramCaptionProps = {
  x: number;
  y: number;
  text: string;
  fill?: string;
  fontSize?: number;
  textAnchor?: "start" | "middle" | "end";
};

export function DiagramCaption({
  x,
  y,
  text,
  fill = "#9ca3af",
  fontSize = 9.5,
  textAnchor = "middle",
}: DiagramCaptionProps) {
  return (
    <text
      x={x}
      y={y}
      fill={fill}
      fontSize={fontSize}
      fontWeight="400"
      textAnchor={textAnchor}
    >
      {text}
    </text>
  );
}

import * as React from "react";

export function ArrowheadDef() {
  return (
    <defs>
      <marker
        id="arrowhead"
        markerWidth="10"
        markerHeight="7"
        refX="0"
        refY="3.5"
        orient="auto"
      >
        <polygon points="0 0, 10 3.5, 0 7" fill="#D9F99D" />
      </marker>
    </defs>
  );
}

```
import * as React from "react";
import {
  DiagramCanvas,
  DiagramGrid,
  DiagramNode,
  DiagramConnection,
  DiagramMarker,
  DiagramCaption,
  ArrowheadDef,
} from "@/components/diagram";

// 1. Overall System Topology
export function OverallSystemDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 220;
  const patternId = "grid-system-overall";
  const nodeY = 80;
  const connectionY = 110;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 60;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Overall System Topology"
      description="Three-node system architecture: Website Portal entry point, Scheduler Core control plane, and Node Network execution plane. Connections show data flow from website to scheduler to compute nodes."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Website */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[WEBSITE_PORTAL]"
        detail="Entry & Onboard"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Control Plane"
      >
        <DiagramMarker cx={125} cy={15} />
      </DiagramNode>

      {/* Node 3: Contributed Nodes */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[NODE_NETWORK]"
        detail="Execution Plane"
      />

      {/* Connections */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth - 45} cy={connectionY} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 2. Request Flow
export function RequestFlowDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 240;
  const patternId = "grid-flow-request";
  const nodeY = 90;
  const connectionY = 120;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Request Flow"
      description="Request lifecycle from client submission through scheduler routing to node execution. Active path highlighted showing successful routing to EU-West node with direct result return path."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Client */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[CLIENT_INTERFACE]"
        detail="Status: SUBMITTING"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Status: ROUTING"
      />

      {/* Node 3: Selected Compute Node */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[NODE_EU_WEST]"
        detail="Status: EXECUTING"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Active Connection Paths */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      {/* Signal indicators on the active loop */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeWidth + 45} cy={connectionY} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 - 45} cy={connectionY} />

      {/* Direct Output Return Path (Subtle feedback loop at bottom) */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 + nodeWidth - 30}
        y1={connectionY + 30}
        x2={startX + 30}
        y2={connectionY + 30}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: width / 2, y: connectionY + 70 }}
      />
      <DiagramCaption
        x={width / 2}
        y={connectionY + 65}
        text="DIRECT_RESULT_PAYLOAD (verification_loop)"
      />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 3. Geographic Scheduling
export function GeographicSchedulingDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 280;
  const patternId = "grid-geo-scheduling";
  const schedulerX = 80;
  const schedulerY = 110;
  const nodeX = 480;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 50;
  const nodeSpacing = 75;
  const startY = 40;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Geographic Scheduling"
      description="Scheduler routing decision showing three candidate nodes with latency measurements. EU-West selected as minimum latency (12ms) vs US-East (78ms) and AP-South (284ms)."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Scheduler Node (Left Column) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={schedulerX}
        y={schedulerY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Latency Engine"
      />

      {/* Nodes (Right Column Stacked) */}
      {/* Node 1: US-East */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_US_EAST]"
        detail="Latency: 78ms"
      />

      {/* Node 2: EU-West (Selected) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY + nodeSpacing}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_EU_WEST]"
        detail="Latency: 12ms (MIN)"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Node 3: AP-South */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY + nodeSpacing * 2}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_AP_SOUTH]"
        detail="Latency: 284ms"
      />

      {/* Routing branches */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeHeight / 2}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: 350, y: 65 }}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeSpacing + nodeHeight / 2}
        active
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeSpacing * 2 + nodeHeight / 2}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: 350, y: 215 }}
      />

      <DiagramMarker cx={350} cy={schedulerY + 30} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 4. Distributed Inference
export function DistributedInferenceDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 280;
  const patternId = "grid-inf-distributed";
  const schedulerX = 80;
  const schedulerY = 110;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 50;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Distributed Inference Pipeline"
      description="Model layer partitioning across three compute shards. Scheduler partitions layers 1-12 to Shard A, 13-24 to Shard B, 25-36 to Shard C. Pipeline flow shown with active connections."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Scheduler (Left) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={schedulerX}
        y={schedulerY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Layer Partitioner"
      />

      {/* Pipeline Shards */}
      {/* Shard A */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={320}
        y={60}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_A]"
        detail="Layers: 1 - 12"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Shard B */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={520}
        y={60}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_B]"
        detail="Layers: 13 - 24"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Shard C */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={420}
        y={170}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeight}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_C]"
        detail="Layers: 25 - 36"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Pipeline connection paths */}
      {/* Scheduler -> Shard A */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={320}
        y2={85}
        active
      />

      {/* Shard A -> Shard B */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={460}
        y1={85}
        x2={520}
        y2={85}
        active
      />

      {/* Shard B -> Shard C */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={590}
        y1={110}
        x2={490}
        y2={170}
        active
      />

      {/* Flow ticks along the pipeline */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={270} cy={112.5} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={490} cy={85} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={540} cy={140} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 5. Future Architecture
export function PlatformStackDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 240;
  const patternId = "grid-stack-platform";
  const layerX = 120;
  const layerWidth = 520;
  const layerHeight = 35;
  const layerSpacing = 45;
  const startY = 30;

  const layers = [
    {
      label: "APPLICATION / API LAYER",
      detail: "Client SDKs, telemetry portals, developer API endpoints",
      y: startY,
      active: false,
    },
    {
      label: "ORCHESTRATION & COORDINATION LAYER",
      detail: "Geographic scheduling engine, node registries, queue models",
      y: startY + layerSpacing,
      active: true,
    },
    {
      label: "DECENTRALIZED TRANSPORT LAYER",
      detail: "P2P overlay routing, message heartbeats, secure gRPC tunnels",
      y: startY + layerSpacing * 2,
      active: false,
    },
    {
      label: "LOCAL HARDWARE EXECUTION RUNTIME",
      detail: "CUDA/ROCm device engines, local resource benchmarks, sandboxes",
      y: startY + layerSpacing * 3,
      active: false,
    },
  ];

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Future Platform Stack Architecture"
      description="Four-layer platform stack: Application API layer, Orchestration & Coordination layer (active), Decentralized Transport layer, and Local Hardware Execution Runtime layer. Each layer spans full width with descriptive details."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {layers.map((layer, index) => (
        <DiagramNode
          key={index}
          x={layerX}
          y={layer.y}
          width={layerWidth}
          height={layerHeight}
          label={layer.label}
          detail={layer.detail}
          active={layer.active}
          detailActive={layer.active}
        />
      ))}
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

src/components/system-diagram.tsx

import * as React from "react";
import {
  DiagramCanvas,
  DiagramGrid,
  DiagramNode,
  DiagramConnection,
  DiagramMarker,
  ArrowheadDef,
} from "@/components/diagram";

export function SystemDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 180;
  const patternId = "grid-home-system";
  const nodeY = 60;
  const connectionY = 90;
  const nodeWidth = 140;
  const nodeHeight = 60;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Public Intelligence System Overview"
      description="Three core components: Website Portal for onboarding, Scheduler Core as coordinator, and Compute Network for execution. Active connection from scheduler to compute network indicated by lime markers."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Website */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[WEBSITE_PORTAL]"
        detail="Role: Onboarding"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Role: Coordinator"
      >
        <DiagramMarker cx={125} cy={15} />
      </DiagramNode>

      {/* Node 3: Global Compute Network */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[COMPUTE_NETWORK]"
        detail="Role: Execution"
      />

      {/* CONNECTIONS (Aligned at Y=90) */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      {/* Data indicator dot */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 - 45} cy={connectionY} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

```
import * as React from "react";
import { PageShell } from "@/components/page-shell";
import { PageHeader } from "@/components/page-header";
import {
  OverallSystemDiagram,
  RequestFlowDiagram,
  GeographicSchedulingDiagram,
  DistributedInferenceDiagram,
  PlatformStackDiagram,
} from "@/components/architecture-diagrams";

export default function ArchitecturePage() {
  return (
    <PageShell>
      <article className="max-w-4xl mx-auto space-y-24">
        <PageHeader
          kicker="System Architecture"
          title="Architecture"
          description="The technical model and system boundaries for distributed AI infrastructure."
        />

        <section className="space-y-16">
          <header className="space-y-4">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-foreground">
              Overall System Topology
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">
              High-level view of the three-plane architecture: the website portal for user onboarding,
              the scheduler core as the control plane, and the contributed node network as the execution plane.
            </p>
          </header>
          <OverallSystemDiagram />
        </section>

        <section className="space-y-16">
          <header className="space-y-4">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-foreground">
              Request Flow
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">
              End-to-end request lifecycle from client submission through scheduler routing to node execution.
              The active path shows successful routing with direct result return bypassing the scheduler for verification.
            </p>
          </header>
          <RequestFlowDiagram />
        </section>

        <section className="space-y-16">
          <header className="space-y-4">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-foreground">
              Geographic Scheduling
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">
              Latency-based node selection across global regions. The scheduler evaluates candidate nodes
              and routes to the minimum-latency target (EU-West at 12ms in this example).
            </p>
          </header>
          <GeographicSchedulingDiagram />
        </section>

        <section className="space-y-16">
          <header className="space-y-4">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-foreground">
              Distributed Inference
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">
              Model layer partitioning across multiple compute shards for large-scale inference.
              Each shard processes a contiguous layer range with pipelined tensor passing.
            </p>
          </header>
          <DistributedInferenceDiagram />
        </section>

        <section className="space-y-16">
          <header className="space-y-4">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-foreground">
              Future Platform Stack
            </h2>
            <p className="text-muted-foreground max-w-3xl">
              Four-layer architecture vision: application APIs, orchestration coordination,
              decentralized transport, and local hardware runtime. The coordination layer is the
              active development focus.
            </p>
          </header>
          <PlatformStackDiagram />
        </section>
      </article>
    </PageShell>
  );
}

# Public Intelligence Website — Design Audit

## Executive Summary

The website demonstrates strong engineering craftsmanship with a clear technical aesthetic. The component architecture is well-organized, the diagram system is sophisticated, and the visual language aligns with the "documentation-first" mandate. However, several high-impact issues undermine the communication of **seriousness, technical credibility, quiet ambition, and long-term institutional thinking**. The most critical gaps are in information hierarchy consistency, diagram accessibility, and responsive behavior at content-critical breakpoints.

---

## 1. Information Hierarchy

### Issue 1.1: Inconsistent Page Header Semantics
**Observed:** `PageHeader` component used across all pages (`vision`, `architecture`, `roadmap`, `contribute`) with `kicker`, `title`, `description` props. However, the home page (`page.tsx`) does not use `PageHeader` — it has a custom hero section with `Logo`, `h1`, and prose. This creates two different "page introduction" patterns.

**Why it matters:** Undermines institutional consistency. Visitors subconsciously learn the site's visual grammar; breaking it on the most important page (home) signals either the home page is special (marketing) or the component system is incomplete.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** Refactor home page to use `PageHeader` with `kicker="Public Intelligence"`, `title="Globally Distributed AI Infrastructure"`, `description="..."` — or extend `PageHeader` to support a `variant="hero"` for the home page while preserving semantic structure.

**Files:** `src/app/page.tsx`, `src/components/page-header.tsx`

---

### Issue 1.2: Missing Section Hierarchy on Content Pages
**Observed:** Pages like `vision/page.tsx` and `architecture/page.tsx` use `<article className="max-w-4xl mx-auto space-y-24">` with only `PageHeader` and then raw content. No consistent section heading component (`<SectionHeader />`) to establish H2/H3 hierarchy.

**Why it matters:** Screen readers and SEO rely on heading hierarchy. Engineers scanning for technical depth need clear section landmarks. Current approach relies on prose `h2`/`h3` which may be inconsistent in spacing, weight, and numbering.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** Create `SectionHeader` component with `level={2|3}`, `kicker?`, `title`, `description?`, `id?` for anchor linking. Enforce `space-y-12` between sections, `space-y-6` within sections.

**Files:** `src/components/section-header.tsx` (new), all page files

---

### Issue 1.3: Roadmap Lacks Temporal Hierarchy
**Observed:** `roadmap/page.tsx` uses `PageHeader` but no visible timeline structure — just prose. A roadmap for "globally distributed AI infrastructure" should communicate *now / next / later* or *quarters / years* visually.

**Why it matters:** "Quiet ambition" requires showing *how* you think about time. A flat list feels like a backlog; a structured timeline feels like an institution.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** Introduce `Timeline` component with `era` (Now/Next/Later or Q1/Q2/Q3/Q4), `items[]` with `title`, `description`, `status` (planned/active/complete). Render as vertical line with markers — consistent with diagram visual language.

**Files:** `src/app/roadmap/page.tsx`, `src/components/timeline.tsx` (new)

---

## 2. Visual Consistency

### Issue 2.1: Inconsistent Container Widths
**Observed:** 
- `PageShell`: `max-w-6xl` (1152px)
- Page articles: `max-w-4xl` (896px)
- Diagrams: `DiagramCanvas` defaults to `width=760` (hardcoded), `ArchitectureDiagram` uses `width=600`, `SystemDiagram` uses `width=760`

**Why it matters:** Content width should be a design token, not per-component decisions. Diagrams wider than prose create horizontal scroll on mobile; narrower diagrams waste space on desktop.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** Define `--container-prose: 48rem` (768px), `--container-wide: 64rem` (1024px), `--container-full: 72rem` (1152px) in `globals.css`. Update `PageShell`, `DiagramCanvas`, all pages to use semantic width classes: `prose-container`, `diagram-container`, `full-container`.

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`, `src/components/page-shell.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`, all page files

---

### Issue 2.2: Color Token Drift in Diagrams
**Observed:** Diagram components use hardcoded colors:
- `DiagramNode`: `stroke="#374151"` (gray-700), `fill="#1f2937"` (gray-800)
- `DiagramConnection`: `stroke="#4b5563"` (gray-600), `active: "#D9F99D"` (lime-300)
- `DiagramMarker`: `fill="#D9F99D"` (lime-300)
- `DiagramGrid`: `stroke="#1f2937"` (gray-800), `pattern` uses `#111827` (gray-900)

**Why it matters:** Hardcoded hex values prevent theming, dark/light mode adaptation, and brand consistency. The lime-300 accent (`#D9F99D`) appears only in diagrams — not in prose, buttons, or links.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** Migrate all diagram colors to CSS custom properties defined in `globals.css`:
```css
:root {
  --diagram-bg: #0f172a;        /* slate-950 */
  --diagram-grid: #1e293b;      /* slate-800 */
  --diagram-node-stroke: #334155; /* slate-700 */
  --diagram-node-fill: #0f172a;  /* slate-950 */
  --diagram-connection: #475569; /* slate-600 */
  --diagram-accent: #D9F99D;     /* lime-300 — keep as brand accent */
  --diagram-text: #94a3b8;       /* slate-400 */
  --diagram-text-muted: #64748b; /* slate-500 */
}
```
Update all diagram components to use `var(--diagram-*)`.

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`, all files in `src/components/diagram/`, `src/components/architecture-diagram.tsx`, `src/components/architecture-diagrams.tsx`, `src/components/system-diagram.tsx`

---

### Issue 2.3: Logo Inconsistency Across Contexts
**Observed:** `Logo` component accepts `className` and `showText`. Used in:
- Home page: `className="w-8 h-8 text-foreground/80"` (no text)
- `PageShell` → `SiteHeader` (not shown, but likely used)
- No favicon/apple-touch-icon integration visible

**Why it matters:** The logo is the primary brand mark. Inconsistent sizing, missing text variant in header, and no favicon strategy weaken institutional identity.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** 
1. Define logo size tokens: `--logo-sm: 2rem`, `--logo-md: 2.5rem`, `--logo-lg: 3rem`
2. Ensure `SiteHeader` uses `Logo` with `showText={true}` on desktop, icon-only on mobile
3. Generate favicon suite from `icon.svg` (32x32, 180x180, 192x192, 512x512, SVG)
4. Add `<link rel="icon" ...>` in `layout.tsx`

**Files:** `src/components/logo.tsx`, `src/components/site-header.tsx`, `src/app/layout.tsx`, `src/app/icon.svg`

---

## 3. Typography

### Issue 3.1: No Explicit Type Scale in CSS
**Observed:** `globals.css` not shown in full, but Tailwind config likely uses default type scale. Pages use arbitrary classes: `text-4xl`, `text-5xl`, `text-lg`, `text-sm`, `text-xs` (in diagrams).

**Why it matters:** "Documentation-first" requires a deliberate type scale with semantic names (e.g., `--text-display`, `--text-h1`, `--text-body`, `--text-caption`, `--text-mono`). Arbitrary Tailwind classes drift over time.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** Define type scale in `globals.css` using `@theme` (Tailwind v4) or `theme.extend` (v3):
```css
@theme {
  --font-sans: "Geist", system-ui, sans-serif;
  --font-mono: "Geist Mono", monospace;
  --text-display: 3.5rem / 1.1;   /* 56px — home hero */
  --text-h1: 2.25rem / 1.2;       /* 36px — page titles */
  --text-h2: 1.5rem / 1.3;        /* 24px — section headers */
  --text-h3: 1.25rem / 1.4;       /* 20px — subsection */
  --text-body: 1rem / 1.7;        /* 16px — prose */
  --text-body-lg: 1.125rem / 1.7; /* 18px — lead paragraphs */
  --text-caption: 0.875rem / 1.5; /* 14px — meta, labels */
  --text-mono: 0.8125rem / 1.6;   /* 13px — code, diagrams */
}
```
Replace all arbitrary `text-*` classes with semantic utilities: `text-display`, `text-h1`, `text-body`, etc.

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`, `tailwind.config.ts` (or `next.config.ts` if using v4), all page and component files

---

### Issue 3.2: Diagram Typography Disconnected from Prose
**Observed:** `DiagramNode` uses `fontSize={11}` (hardcoded), `DiagramCaption` uses `fontSize={9.5}`. Prose uses `text-base` (16px). No relationship.

**Why it matters:** Diagrams are not illustrations — they are technical documentation. Their type must harmonize with body text for cognitive continuity.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** 
1. Set diagram base font size to `var(--text-mono)` (13px)
2. `DiagramNode` label: `var(--text-caption)` (14px, medium)
3. `DiagramNode` detail: `var(--text-mono)` (13px, regular)
4. `DiagramCaption`: `calc(var(--text-mono) * 0.85)` ≈ 11px
5. Pass `fontSize` as prop defaulting to CSS variable, not hardcoded number

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramCaption.tsx`, `src/app/globals.css`

---

### Issue 3.3: Missing Monospace Consistency
**Observed:** `DiagramNode` and `DiagramCaption` don't specify `font-family`. Prose likely uses sans. Technical labels (node names, captions) should be monospace.

**Why it matters:** Monospace for technical identifiers (service names, protocols, paths) improves scannability and signals precision.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** Add `font-family: var(--font-mono)` to `DiagramNode` label/detail, `DiagramCaption`, `DiagramMarker` tooltips (if any).

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramCaption.tsx`

---

## 4. Whitespace and Spacing

### Issue 4.1: Magic Numbers in Diagram Layouts
**Observed:** `architecture-diagrams.tsx` and `system-diagram.tsx` contain extensive hardcoded layout constants:
```ts
const width = 760;
const height = 220;
const nodeY = 80;
const connectionY = 110;
const nodeWidth = 140;
const nodeHeight = 60;
const nodeSpacing = 230;
const startX = 80;
```

**Why it matters:** These are not responsive. On mobile (< 760px), diagrams overflow or require horizontal scroll. No adaptation for narrow viewports.

**Impact:** **Critical**

**Solution:** 
1. Make `DiagramCanvas` responsive: `width="100%"`, `viewBox="0 0 760 220"`, `preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"`
2. Replace magic numbers with relative units in diagram components (e.g., `nodeSpacing = width / 3.3`)
3. For complex diagrams, provide mobile-specific layouts (stacked nodes) via `useMediaQuery` or CSS container queries
4. Add `overflow-x: auto` wrapper only as last resort — prefer reflow

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`, `src/components/architecture-diagrams.tsx`, `src/components/system-diagram.tsx`, `src/components/architecture-diagram.tsx`

---

### Issue 4.2: Inconsistent Vertical Rhythm
**Observed:** 
- `PageShell`: `py-20 sm:py-24` (80px / 96px)
- Page articles: `space-y-24` (96px) or `space-y-20` (80px)
- `PageHeader`: internal spacing not visible
- Diagrams: `my-12` (48px) in `ArchitectureDiagram`

**Why it matters:** Vertical rhythm should derive from a base unit (e.g., 4px or 8px) and scale consistently. Current values (20, 24, 12) suggest ad-hoc decisions.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** Define spacing scale in `globals.css`:
```css
@theme {
  --space-1: 0.25rem;   /* 4px */
  --space-2: 0.5rem;    /* 8px */
  --space-3: 1rem;      /* 16px */
  --space-4: 1.5rem;    /* 24px */
  --space-5: 2rem;      /* 32px */
  --space-6: 3rem;      /* 48px */
  --space-7: 4rem;      /* 64px */
  --space-8: 6rem;      /* 96px */
}
```
Map: `PageShell` padding → `py-6 sm:py-7`, article `space-y-8`, diagram `my-5`.

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`, `src/components/page-shell.tsx`, all page files, diagram components

---

### Issue 4.3: Diagram Internal Spacing Not Systematic
**Observed:** `DiagramNode` uses fixed `width=140`, `height=60`, `rx=4`. `DiagramCaption` at `y` offset. No padding tokens inside nodes.

**Why it matters:** Node content (label + detail) needs consistent internal padding. Current `x+12`, `y+20` hardcoded in `DiagramNode`.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** Add `--diagram-node-padding: 1rem` (16px), `--diagram-node-gap: 0.5rem` (8px) to CSS. Use in `DiagramNode` for text positioning.

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`

---

## 5. Component Consistency

### Issue 5.1: Duplicate Diagram Implementations
**Observed:** Three diagram systems coexist:
1. `architecture-diagram.tsx` — standalone SVG, 600x300, different node style
2. `architecture-diagrams.tsx` — uses `DiagramCanvas`, `DiagramNode`, `DiagramConnection` (shared components)
3. `system-diagram.tsx` — similar to #2 but different constants, used on home page

**Why it matters:** Maintenance burden, visual drift, inconsistent behavior (responsiveness, accessibility). `architecture-diagram.tsx` appears abandoned.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** 
1. Audit which diagrams are actually used (check imports in pages)
2. Migrate all to shared `DiagramCanvas` + `DiagramNode` + `DiagramConnection` system
3. Delete `architecture-diagram.tsx` if unused
4. Ensure `system-diagram.tsx` uses same constants/tokens as `architecture-diagrams.tsx`

**Files:** `src/components/architecture-diagram.tsx`, `src/components/architecture-diagrams.tsx`, `src/components/system-diagram.tsx`, `src/app/page.tsx`, `src/app/architecture/page.tsx`

---

### Issue 5.2: `PageShell` Includes Footer but Not Header
**Observed:** `PageShell` renders `children` + `SiteFooter`. `SiteHeader` is not included — likely rendered in `layout.tsx` or per-page.

**Why it matters:** Inconsistent page shell contract. Every page should have identical chrome (header, main, footer) unless explicitly opted out.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** Move `SiteHeader` into `PageShell` (before `children`). Update `layout.tsx` to use `PageShell` as sole wrapper. Pages that need no header (unlikely) can opt out via prop.

**Files:** `src/components/page-shell.tsx`, `src/app/layout.tsx`, `src/components/site-header.tsx`

---

### Issue 5.3: No Shared Prose/Content Component
**Observed:** Pages use raw `<p>`, `<h2>`, `<ul>`, `<code>` with Tailwind classes. No `Prose` or `Content` component to enforce consistent typography, spacing, code styling, link styling.

**Why it matters:** "Documentation-first" requires predictable rendering of Markdown-like content. Current approach leads to drift (e.g., `text-foreground/70` vs `text-muted-foreground`, inconsistent `code` styling).

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** Create `Prose` component (wrapper for `prose` Tailwind plugin or custom styles) with:
- Semantic heading sizes (`h2` → `text-h2`, `h3` → `text-h3`)
- Consistent `code`/`pre` styling (monospace, bg, padding)
- Link styling (underline on hover, external icon)
- List spacing
- Table styling (if needed)

**Files:** `src/components/prose.tsx` (new), all page files

---

## 6. Diagram Quality

### Issue 6.1: Diagrams Lack Accessibility (Critical)
**Observed:** All diagrams are inline `<svg>` with no:
- `<title>` / `<desc>` for screen readers
- `role="img"` + `aria-labelledby`
- Text alternatives for node/connection semantics
- Keyboard navigation (focusable elements)
- High-contrast mode support

**Why it matters:** Diagrams convey core architecture. Inaccessible diagrams exclude blind/low-vision engineers — violating both ethics and the "public infrastructure" mission.

**Impact:** **Critical**

**Solution:** 
1. `DiagramCanvas` must accept `title`, `description` (already has props!) and render:
```tsx
<svg ... role="img" aria-labelledby={titleId} aria-describedby={descId}>
  <title id={titleId}>{title}</title>
  <desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>
  ...
</svg>
```
2. Each `DiagramNode` → `<g role="graphics-symbol" aria-roledescription="node" aria-label={label}>`
3. Each `DiagramConnection` → `<g role="graphics-symbol" aria-roledescription="connection" aria-label={`${from} to ${to}`}>`
4. Add `focusable` elements for keyboard traversal (optional but recommended)
5. Test with NVDA/VoiceOver

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx`, all diagram usage sites

---

### Issue 6.2: Diagram Interactivity Missing
**Observed:** `DiagramNode` has `active` and `detailActive` props but no visible interactivity (hover, focus, click). `DiagramConnection` has `active` prop.

**Why it matters:** If diagrams support `active` state, they should be interactive — e.g., click node to highlight connections, show detail panel. Static diagrams with unused interactive props are confusing.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** 
1. Decide: are diagrams interactive or static?
2. If static: remove `active`, `detailActive` props
3. If interactive: implement hover/focus states, click handlers, detail panel (sidecar or tooltip), keyboard support
4. Document in `DiagramCanvas` props

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`

---

### Issue 6.3: Arrowhead Definition Duplicated
**Observed:** `ArrowheadDef` component defines `<marker id="arrowhead">`. Used in `DiagramConnection` via `marker-end="url(#arrowhead)"`. But `architecture-diagram.tsx` has its own inline `<defs><marker id="arrowhead">...</marker></defs>`.

**Why it matters:** Duplicate definitions cause ID collisions if multiple diagrams on same page. Violates DRY.

**Impact:** **Low**

**Solution:** Ensure `ArrowheadDef` is rendered once per page (e.g., in `DiagramCanvas` or `layout.tsx`). Remove inline defs from `architecture-diagram.tsx`.

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/ArrowheadDef.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`, `src/components/architecture-diagram.tsx`

---

### Issue 6.4: Grid Pattern ID Collisions
**Observed:** `DiagramGrid` accepts `patternId` prop. `architecture-diagrams.tsx` uses `"grid-system-overall"`, `system-diagram.tsx` uses `"grid-home-system"`. If both diagrams render on same page (unlikely but possible), IDs must be unique.

**Why it matters:** SVG `id` must be unique per document. Current approach relies on manual uniqueness.

**Impact:** **Low**

**Solution:** Auto-generate `patternId` in `DiagramGrid` using `useId()` or `crypto.randomUUID()` suffix. Or render `DiagramGrid` inside `DiagramCanvas` which provides unique namespace.

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramGrid.tsx`, `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`

---

## 7. Accessibility

### Issue 7.1: Missing Skip Link
**Observed:** No "Skip to main content" link in `layout.tsx` or `PageShell`.

**Why it matters:** Keyboard users must tab through header navigation on every page. Required for WCAG 2.1 AA.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** Add in `PageShell` (first child):
```tsx
<a href="#main-content" className="sr-only focus:not-sr-only focus:absolute focus:top-4 focus:left-4 z-50 px-4 py-2 bg-background text-foreground">
  Skip to main content
</a>
<main id="main-content" ...>{children}</main>
```

**Files:** `src/components/page-shell.tsx`

---

### Issue 7.2: Color Contrast Unverified
**Observed:** Diagram colors (slate-950 bg, slate-400 text, lime-300 accent) — contrast ratios not verified. Prose uses `text-foreground/70`, `text-muted-foreground` — depends on `globals.css` definitions.

**Why it matters:** Technical content read for long periods. Low contrast causes fatigue, excludes low-vision users.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** 
1. Audit all color pairs in `globals.css` against WCAG AA (4.5:1 normal, 3:1 large)
2. Ensure `--diagram-text` (slate-400) on `--diagram-bg` (slate-950) ≥ 4.5:1
3. Ensure `--diagram-accent` (lime-300) on `--diagram-bg` ≥ 3:1 (for UI elements)
4. Document contrast ratios in `STYLE_GUIDE.md`

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`, `docs/STYLE_GUIDE.md`

---

### Issue 7.3: Reduced Motion Not Respected
**Observed:** No `prefers-reduced-motion` media query in CSS. Diagrams have no animation currently, but future transitions (node highlight, connection flow) would need it.

**Why it matters:** Vestibular disorders. Proactive compliance.

**Impact:** **Low**

**Solution:** Add to `globals.css`:
```css
@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce) {
  *, *::before, *::after {
    animation-duration: 0.01ms !important;
    animation-iteration-count: 1 !important;
    transition-duration: 0.01ms !important;
    scroll-behavior: auto !important;
  }
}
```

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`

---

## 8. Responsiveness

### Issue 8.1: Diagrams Not Responsive (Critical)
**Observed:** `DiagramCanvas` has fixed `width=760`, `height=240` defaults. `viewBox` matches. No `width="100%"` or `max-width: 100%`. On mobile (375px), diagram overflows.

**Why it matters:** Architecture diagrams are core content. Horizontal scroll on mobile breaks reading flow, hides context.

**Impact:** **Critical**

**Solution:** 
1. `DiagramCanvas` SVG: `width="100%"`, `height="auto"`, `max-width: 100%`, `viewBox="0 0 {width} {height}"`
2. Wrapper `div`: `overflow-x: auto` only as fallback (with scroll shadow indicator)
3. For complex diagrams, provide `mobileLayout` prop to `DiagramCanvas` that rearranges nodes vertically

**Files:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`, all diagram usage sites

---

### Issue 8.2: Home Page Hero Not Mobile-Optimized
**Observed:** `page.tsx` hero: `text-4xl sm:text-5xl md:text-6xl`, `max-w-3xl`. Logo `w-8 h-8`. On mobile, `text-4xl` (36px) may be too large for `max-w-3xl` (48rem) — but container is `max-w-4xl` (896px) in article.

**Why it matters:** First impression. Oversized hero text on mobile pushes diagram below fold.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** 
1. Reduce mobile hero: `text-3xl sm:text-4xl md:text-5xl lg:text-6xl`
2. Ensure `Logo` scales: `w-6 h-6 sm:w-8 sm:h-8`
3. Add `prose-container` class to hero wrapper

**Files:** `src/app/page.tsx`, `src/components/logo.tsx`

---

### Issue 8.3: Navigation Not Mobile-Adaptive
**Observed:** `SiteHeader` not shown, but likely contains navigation. No mobile menu pattern visible.

**Why it matters:** 5+ pages (Home, Vision, Architecture, Research, Roadmap, Contribute) — needs responsive nav.

**Impact:** **High**

**Solution:** 
1. `SiteHeader`: desktop = horizontal nav, mobile = drawer/sheet (Radix UI or headless)
2. Include logo with text on desktop, icon-only on mobile
3. Ensure keyboard accessible

**Files:** `src/components/site-header.tsx`, `src/components/logo.tsx`

---

## 9. Overall Craftsmanship

### Issue 9.1: No Print Stylesheet
**Observed:** No `@media print` styles. Technical pages (Architecture, Vision, Roadmap) will be printed/PDF'd by engineers.

**Why it matters:** "Documentation-first" includes print. Diagrams, code, tables must render cleanly.

**Impact:** **Medium**

**Solution:** Add to `globals.css`:
```css
@media print {
  .no-print { display: none !important; }
  main { max-width: none; padding: 0; }
  .prose { font-size: 11pt; line-height: 1.6; }
  svg { max-width: 100% !important; page-break-inside: avoid; }
  a::after { content: " (" attr(href) ")"; font-size: 0.8em; color: #666; }
}
```
Mark `SiteHeader`, `SiteFooter`, interactive elements with `no-print`.

**Files:** `src/app/globals.css`, `src/components/page-shell.tsx`, `src/components/site-header.tsx`, `src/components/site-footer.tsx`

---

### Issue 9.2: No Content Integrity Checks
**Observed:** No automated checks for:
- Broken internal links (anchor `href="#section"` vs `id="section"`)
- Missing `alt` on images (only logo/icon)
- Diagram accessibility attributes
- Heading hierarchy (h1 → h2 → h3)

**Why it matters:** Craftsmanship includes tooling to prevent regressions.

**Impact:** **Low**

**Solution:** Add to CI:
1. `markdown-link-check` for `.md` docs
2. Custom script for `.tsx` anchor links
3. `axe-core` in Playwright for a11y
4. `remark-lint` heading hierarchy

**Files:** `package.json`, `.github/workflows/` (new), `docs/DEVELOPMENT.md`

---

### Issue 9.3: Favicon / PWA Manifest Missing
**Observed:** `icon.svg` exists but no `<link rel="icon">`, `manifest.json`, `apple-touch-icon`.

**Why it matters:** Institutional credibility. "Public Intelligence" should install as PWA, have proper icons.

**Impact:** **Low**

**Solution:** 
1. Generate icons from `icon.svg`: 16, 32, 48, 72, 96, 128, 144, 152, 180, 192, 512
2. Add `public/manifest.json` with name, icons, theme_color
3. Add `<link rel="icon" sizes="any" href="/icon.svg">` + PNG fallbacks in `layout.tsx`

**Files:** `src/app/layout.tsx`, `public/manifest.json` (new), `public/icons/` (new)

---

## Next Steps

This audit identifies **27 issues** across 9 criteria. The top 5 (Critical/High) should be addressed before public launch:

1. **Responsive diagrams** — core content must work on mobile
2. **Diagram accessibility** — non-negotiable for public infrastructure
3. **Design token system** — colors, type, spacing as CSS variables
4. **Shared Prose component** — enforce documentation quality
5. **Mobile navigation** — basic usability

I recommend tackling in this order, with each change verified by:
- `npm run build` (no errors)
- Mobile viewport testing (375px, 768px, 1440px)
- Axe-core accessibility scan
- Print preview check

## Phase 3 — Implementation Plan: Top 5 Critical/High Issues

### 1. Responsive Diagrams (`DiagramCanvas.tsx` + all diagram files)

**Files to modify:**
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`
- `src/components/architecture-diagrams.tsx`
- `src/components/system-diagram.tsx`
- `src/components/architecture-diagram.tsx` (if kept)

**Exact changes:**
- `DiagramCanvas` SVG: add `width="100%" height="auto" max-width="100%"` and `preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"`
- Remove fixed `width`/`height` from SVG element; keep `viewBox` for aspect ratio
- Wrapper `div`: add `overflow-x: auto` with scroll shadow indicator (CSS `::-webkit-scrollbar` hidden, shadow via `box-shadow`)
- All diagram components: replace magic numbers with relative calculations based on `viewBox` width (e.g., `nodeSpacing = width / 3.3`)

**Why:** Fixed 760px diagrams overflow on mobile (375px). Core architecture content must be readable without horizontal scroll.

**Accessibility:** `overflow-x: auto` wrapper must be keyboard-focusable (`tabindex="0"`) with visible focus ring for scroll discovery.

**Responsiveness:** Diagrams scale fluidly from 320px to 1440px+. Complex diagrams (Geographic Scheduling, Distributed Inference) may need `mobileLayout` prop for stacked node arrangement.

**Reusability:** `DiagramCanvas` becomes the single responsive container for all diagrams.

---

### 2. Diagram Accessibility (`DiagramCanvas.tsx`, `DiagramNode.tsx`, `DiagramConnection.tsx`)

**Files to modify:**
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx`

**Exact changes:**
- `DiagramCanvas`: render `<title id={titleId}>{title}</title>` and `<desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>`; SVG gets `role="img" aria-labelledby={titleId} aria-describedby={descId}`
- `DiagramNode`: wrap content in `<g role="graphics-symbol" aria-roledescription="node" aria-label={`${label}: ${detail}`}>`; add `tabIndex={0}` for keyboard focus
- `DiagramConnection`: wrap in `<g role="graphics-symbol" aria-roledescription="connection" aria-label={`Connection from ${from} to ${to}`}>` (requires `from`/`to` props)
- Add CSS for focus visible: `[role="graphics-symbol"]:focus { outline: 2px solid var(--diagram-accent); outline-offset: 2px; }`

**Why:** Diagrams convey core architecture. Screen reader users currently get no semantic information. WCAG 2.1 AA requires non-text content alternatives.

**Accessibility:** Full keyboard traversal of nodes/connections. `aria-roledescription` provides SVG-specific semantics. Focus management enables exploration.

**Responsiveness:** No impact — accessibility attributes are viewport-agnostic.

**Reusability:** All diagrams automatically gain accessibility when using shared components.

---

### 3. Design Token System (`globals.css` + all diagram components)

**Files to modify:**
- `src/app/globals.css`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramGrid.tsx`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramMarker.tsx`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramCaption.tsx`
- `src/components/architecture-diagrams.tsx`
- `src/components/system-diagram.tsx`
- `src/components/architecture-diagram.tsx`

**Exact changes:**
In `globals.css`, add to `:root`:
```css
/* Diagram tokens */
--diagram-bg: oklch(0.145 0 0);           /* matches --background */
--diagram-grid: oklch(0.205 0 0);         /* matches --card */
--diagram-node-stroke: oklch(0.371 0 0);  /* slate-700 */
--diagram-node-fill: oklch(0.145 0 0);    /* matches --background */
--diagram-connection: oklch(0.439 0 0);   /* slate-600 */
--diagram-accent: #D9F99D;                /* lime-300 — brand accent */
--diagram-text: oklch(0.708 0 0);         /* matches --muted-foreground */
--diagram-text-muted: oklch(0.556 0 0);   /* matches --ring */
--diagram-node-padding: 1rem;             /* 16px */
--diagram-node-gap: 0.5rem;               /* 8px */
--diagram-node-radius: 0.25rem;           /* 4px */
--diagram-stroke-width: 1px;
--diagram-stroke-width-active: 1.2px;
```

Replace all hardcoded colors in diagram components with `var(--diagram-*)`.

**Why:** Hardcoded hex values prevent theming, drift from prose colors, and make maintenance fragile. Tokens align diagrams with global design system.

**Accessibility:** Tokens enable high-contrast mode overrides via `@media (prefers-contrast: high)`.

**Responsiveness:** No direct impact, but tokens can have responsive variants if needed.

**Reusability:** Single source of truth for all diagram visual properties.

---

### 4. Type Scale (`globals.css` + component updates)

**Files to modify:**
- `src/app/globals.css`
- `src/components/page-header.tsx`
- `src/components/page-shell.tsx`
- `src/app/page.tsx`
- `src/app/vision/page.tsx`
- `src/app/architecture/page.tsx`
- `src/app/roadmap/page.tsx`
- `src/app/contribute/page.tsx`
- `src/app/research/page.tsx`

**Exact changes:**
In `globals.css`, add to `@theme`:
```css
@theme {
  --font-sans: var(--font-geist);
  --font-mono: var(--font-geist);
  --text-display: 3.5rem / 1.1;      /* 56px — home hero */
  --text-h1: 2.25rem / 1.2;          /* 36px — page titles */
  --text-h2: 1.5rem / 1.3;           /* 24px — section headers */
  --text-h3: 1.25rem / 1.4;          /* 20px — subsection */
  --text-body: 1rem / 1.7;           /* 16px — prose */
  --text-body-lg: 1.125rem / 1.7;    /* 18px — lead paragraphs */
  --text-caption: 0.875rem / 1.5;    /* 14px — meta, labels */
  --text-mono: 0.8125rem / 1.6;      /* 13px — code, diagrams */
}
```

Replace arbitrary `text-*` classes:
- `PageHeader` title → `text-h1`
- `PageHeader` description → `text-body-lg`
- Page `h2` → `text-h2`
- Page `h3` → `text-h3`
- Prose `p` → `text-body`
- Meta/kicker text → `text-caption font-mono uppercase tracking-wider`

**Why:** Arbitrary Tailwind classes drift. Semantic type scale ensures consistency, enables global changes, and communicates hierarchy intentionally.

**Accessibility:** Relative units (`rem`) respect user font-size preferences. Line heights meet WCAG 1.4.12 (text spacing).

**Responsiveness:** Type scale can have responsive variants (e.g., `--text-display-mobile: 2.5rem`) via `@media` in CSS.

**Reusability:** All pages and components use shared scale. New pages inherit correct hierarchy automatically.

---

### 5. Diagram Typography Alignment (`DiagramNode.tsx`, `DiagramCaption.tsx`, `globals.css`)

**Files to modify:**
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`
- `src/components/diagram/DiagramCaption.tsx`
- `src/app/globals.css` (uses tokens from #3 and #4)

**Exact changes:**
- `DiagramNode` label: `font-size: var(--text-caption)` (14px), `font-weight: 600`, `font-family: var(--font-mono)`, `fill: var(--diagram-text)`
- `DiagramNode` detail: `font-size: var(--text-mono)` (13px), `font-weight: 400`, `font-family: var(--font-mono)`, `fill: var(--diagram-text-muted)`
- `DiagramCaption`: `font-size: calc(var(--text-mono) * 0.85)` (~11px), `font-family: var(--font-mono)`, `fill: var(--diagram-text-muted)`
- Remove hardcoded `fontSize` props; use CSS variables with `style={{ fontSize: 'var(--text-caption)' }}` or class-based approach
- Text positioning: use `var(--diagram-node-padding)` and `var(--diagram-node-gap)` for `x`/`y` offsets

**Why:** Diagram text currently uses hardcoded 11px/9.5px with no font-family. Technical labels (service names, protocols) must be monospace and harmonize with prose for cognitive continuity.

**Accessibility:** Monospace improves readability for technical identifiers. Relative sizing respects user preferences.

**Responsiveness:** Diagram text scales with `--text-mono` if responsive type scale is implemented.

**Reusability:** `DiagramNode` and `DiagramCaption` become fully token-driven — no magic numbers.

Now I have all necessary files. I'll begin implementation with **Priority 1: Responsive Diagrams** starting with `DiagramCanvas.tsx`.

src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx
````
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramCanvasProps = {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  className?: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
};

export function DiagramCanvas({
  children,
  width = 760,
  height = 240,
  className = "",
  title,
  description,
}: DiagramCanvasProps) {
  const titleId = `diagram-title-${React.useId()}`;
  const descId = `diagram-desc-${React.useId()}`;
  const gridId = `grid-${React.useId()}`;

  return (
    <div className={`w-full flex justify-center py-4 ${className}`} tabindex="0" role="region" aria-label={title}>
      <svg
        viewBox={`0 0 ${width} ${height}`}
        fill="none"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        className="w-full max-w-4xl font-mono"
        role="img"
        aria-labelledby={titleId}
        aria-describedby={descId}
        preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"
        style={{ width: "100%", height: "auto", maxWidth: "100%" }}
      >
        <title id={titleId}>{title}</title>
        <desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>
        <defs>
          <pattern
            id={gridId}
            width="20"
            height="20"
            patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse"
          >
            <path
              d="M 20 0 L 0 0 0 20"
              fill="none"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="0.5"
              strokeOpacity="0.03"
            />
          </pattern>
          <marker
            id="arrowhead"
            markerWidth="10"
            markerHeight="7"
            refX="0"
            refY="3.5"
            orient="auto"
          >
            <polygon points="0 0, 10 3.5, 0 7" fill="var(--diagram-accent, #D9F99D)" />
          </marker>
        </defs>
        <rect
          width={width}
          height={height}
          fill={`url(#${gridId})`}
          rx="6"
        />
        {children}
      </svg>
      <style jsx>{`
        div:focus-visible {
          outline: 2px solid var(--diagram-accent, #D9F99D);
          outline-offset: 4px;
          border-radius: 6px;
        }
      `}</style>
    </div>
  );
}
````

 import * as React from "react";
 
 type DiagramNodeProps = {
   x: number;
   y: number;
   width?: number;
   height?: number;
   rx?: number;
   label: string;
   detail?: string;
   active?: boolean;
   detailActive?: boolean;
   className?: string;
 };
 
 export function DiagramNode({
   x,
   y,
   width = 140,
   height = 60,
   rx = 4,
   label,
   detail,
   active = false,
   detailActive = false,
   className = "",
 }: DiagramNodeProps) {
   const nodeId = `node-${React.useId()}`;
   const isActive = active || detailActive;
 
   return (
     <g
       role="graphics-symbol"
       aria-roledescription="node"
       aria-label={detail ? `${label}: ${detail}` : label}
       tabIndex={0}
       className="focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-[var(--diagram-accent)] focus-visible:ring-offset-2 focus-visible:ring-offset-[var(--diagram-bg)]"
     >
       <rect
         x={x}
         y={y}
         width={width}
         height={height}
         rx={rx}
         fill="var(--diagram-node-fill)"
         stroke={isActive ? "var(--diagram-accent)" : "var(--diagram-node-stroke)"}
         strokeWidth={isActive ? "var(--diagram-stroke-width-active)" : "var(--diagram-stroke-width)"}
         className={className}
       />
       <text
         x={x + 16}
         y={y + 22}
         fontSize="var(--text-caption)"
         fontWeight={600}
         fontFamily="var(--font-mono)"
         fill="var(--diagram-text)"
         style={{ fontSize: "var(--text-caption)", fontFamily: "var(--font-mono)" }}
       >
         {label}
       </text>
       {detail && (
         <text
           x={x + 16}
           y={y + 42}
           fontSize="var(--text-mono)"
           fontWeight={400}
           fontFamily="var(--font-mono)"
           fill="var(--diagram-text-muted)"
           style={{ fontSize: "var(--text-mono)", fontFamily: "var(--font-mono)" }}
         >
           {detail}
         </text>
       )}
     </g>
   );
 }

The issue is that diagrams have fixed widths (760px) and don't scale on mobile. The DiagramCanvas needs to be responsive.

Let me read the current DiagramCanvas implementation first to understand what needs to change.

From the provided files, I can see:

**DiagramCanvas.tsx** - Currently has fixed width/height, uses viewBox but the SVG doesn't have `width="100%" height="auto" max-width="100%"` and `preserveAspectRatio`. The wrapper div doesn't have overflow handling.

**architecture-diagrams.tsx** - All diagrams use hardcoded width=760, height=220/240/280, and magic numbers for positioning.

**system-diagram.tsx** - Same issue, hardcoded width=760, height=180.

**architecture-diagram.tsx** - Different implementation, uses fixed width="600" height="300" on SVG directly.

The key changes needed:
1. DiagramCanvas: Make SVG responsive with width="100%" height="auto" max-width="100%" and preserveAspectRatio
2. Add overflow-x: auto wrapper with scroll shadow for fallback
3. The diagram components (architecture-diagrams, system-diagram) use magic numbers but those are based on the viewBox coordinates, so they should scale automatically if the viewBox is preserved. The issue is just the container responsiveness.

Wait, looking more carefully at the diagrams - they use absolute coordinates (x, y positions) based on the fixed width/height. If we make the SVG responsive with viewBox, the coordinates will scale proportionally, which is what we want. The magic numbers are in viewBox coordinate space, not pixel space.

So the main fix is in DiagramCanvas.tsx - making the SVG element responsive. The diagram components don't need to change their coordinate calculations because they're already using the viewBox coordinate system.

Let me verify: In architecture-diagrams.tsx, they pass width=760, height=220 to DiagramCanvas, and then use those same numbers for positioning (startX=80, nodeSpacing=230, etc.). These are viewBox coordinates. So if the SVG scales, everything scales proportionally.

The fix is primarily in DiagramCanvas.tsx. But I should also check if any diagram components have hardcoded pixel values that won't scale.

Looking at DiagramNode.tsx - it uses x, y props which are passed in viewBox coordinates. The width/height are also in viewBox coordinates. So it should scale.

DiagramConnection - same, uses x1, y1, x2, y2 in viewBox coordinates.

DiagramGrid - uses width/height in viewBox coordinates for the rect.

DiagramMarker - uses cx, cy in viewBox coordinates.

DiagramCaption - uses x, y in viewBox coordinates.

So all diagram components work in viewBox coordinate space. The only issue is the DiagramCanvas SVG element not being responsive.

However, there's also the issue of the grid pattern - it uses a fixed pattern size (20x20) which is in userSpaceOnUse units, so it will scale with the viewBox.

The ArrowheadDef is defined in DiagramCanvas now (I see it was moved there in the updated version), which is good.

Now, the user said "Modify only the minimum number of files required." So I should only change DiagramCanvas.tsx to make it responsive.

But wait - the user also said "Preserve the existing visual appearance on desktop." So on desktop, it should look the same (760px wide). The max-w-4xl class on the SVG limits it to 896px (max-w-4xl = 896px), but the viewBox is 760. So on desktop, it should render at 760px (or up to 896px if the container is wider).

Actually, looking at the current DiagramCanvas:
- SVG has `className="w-full max-w-4xl font-mono"`
- viewBox is `0 0 ${width} ${height}` where width=760 by default
- The wrapper div is `w-full flex justify-center py-4`

So on desktop, the SVG will be 760px (since viewBox width is 760 and it's w-full but constrained by max-w-4xl which is 896px > 760px). On mobile, w-full will make it try to fill the container, but without height:auto and preserveAspectRatio, it might not scale properly.

The fix: Add `width="100%" height="auto" max-width="100%"` and `preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"` to the SVG. Also add overflow handling to the wrapper.

Let me also check if there's a style jsx for focus-visible that was added in the previous commit.
