```tsx
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramCanvasProps = {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  className?: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
};

export function DiagramCanvas({
  children,
  width = 760,
  height = 240,
  className = "",
  title,
  description,
}: DiagramCanvasProps) {
  const titleId = `diagram-title-${React.useId()}`;
  const descId = `diagram-desc-${React.useId()}`;

  return (
    <div className={`w-full flex justify-center py-4 ${className}`}>
      <svg
        viewBox={`0 0 ${width} ${height}`}
        fill="none"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        className="w-full max-w-4xl font-mono"
        role="img"
        aria-labelledby={titleId}
        aria-describedby={descId}
      >
        <title id={titleId}>{title}</title>
        <desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>
        <defs>
          <pattern
            id={`grid-${React.useId()}`}
            width="20"
            height="20"
            patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse"
          >
            <path
              d="M 20 0 L 0 0 0 20"
              fill="none"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="0.5"
              strokeOpacity="0.03"
            />
          </pattern>
        </defs>
        <rect
          width={width}
          height={height}
          fill={`url(#grid-${React.useId()})`}
          rx="6"
        />
        {children}
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}
```

Also, I need to consider: the wrapper currently has `className="w-full flex justify-center py-4"`. The `justify-center` centers the SVG. With `overflow-x: auto`, we probably don't want `justify-center` because on mobile the SVG will be narrower than the container. Actually, `w-full` on the wrapper makes it full width. The SVG has `max-w-4xl` (896px) and `w-full`. On mobile, the container is < 760px, so the SVG will be constrained by the container width. The `justify-center` doesn't hurt.

But with `overflow-x: auto`, if the SVG is wider than the container (which it won't be with `max-width: 100%`), it would scroll. But with `max-width: 100%`, the SVG will never be wider than the container. So `overflow-x: auto` is actually not needed if we set `max-width: 100%` on the SVG!

Wait, that's the key: if the SVG has `max-width: 100%` and `width: 100%`, it will scale down to fit the container. No horizontal scroll needed. The `overflow-x: auto` is only a fallback if for some reason the SVG exceeds the container.

But the viewBox is 760px wide. On a 375px mobile screen, the SVG will scale to 375px (100% of container), and the content will scale proportionally. This is exactly what we want.

So the fix is simply:
1. SVG: `width="100%" height="auto" max-width="100%" preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"`
2. Keep the wrapper as is (or add `overflow-x: auto` as safety)

Actually, in SVG, `width` and `height` attributes can be set to "100%" and "auto". But `max-width` is a CSS property. So better to use `style={{ width: "100%", height: "auto", maxWidth: "100%" }}`.

And `preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"` ensures it scales proportionally centered.

## Analysis

**Files involved in diagram rendering:**
1. `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx` - Root SVG container (shared by all diagrams)
2. `src/components/architecture-diagrams.tsx` - 5 architecture diagrams (OverallSystem, RequestFlow, GeographicScheduling, DistributedInference, PlatformStack)
3. `src/components/system-diagram.tsx` - Home page system diagram
4. `src/components/architecture-diagram.tsx` - Standalone legacy diagram (unused in current pages)

**Rendering hierarchy:**
```
Page (architecture/page.tsx, page.tsx)
  → Diagram Component (architecture-diagrams.tsx, system-diagram.tsx)
    → DiagramCanvas (shared)
      → SVG with viewBox
      → DiagramGrid, DiagramNode, DiagramConnection, DiagramMarker, DiagramCaption
```

**Current problem:** `DiagramCanvas` SVG lacks responsive attributes. It has `viewBox` but no `width="100%" height="auto" max-width="100%" preserveAspectRatio`, so on mobile. All child components use viewBox coordinates (magic numbers like 760, 230, 80) which scale proportionally when viewBox is preserved.

**Only file requiring change:** `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx` - the single shared SVG container. All diagram components pass width/height as viewBox dimensions; they don't need modification.

**Why no other files:** 
- Diagram components (`architecture-diagrams.tsx`, `system-diagram.tsx`) use viewBox-relative coordinates
- `architecture-diagram.tsx` is unused (not imported by any page)
- No typography, color, or accessibility changes needed

---

## Implementation

src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx
````
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramCanvasProps = {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  className?: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
};

export function DiagramCanvas({
  children,
  width = 760,
  height = 240,
  className = "",
  title,
  description,
}: DiagramCanvasProps) {
  const titleId = `diagram-title-${React.useId()}`;
  const descId = `diagram-desc-${React.useId()}`;
  const gridId = `grid-${React.useId()}`;

  return (
    <div className={`w-full flex justify-center py-4 ${className}`} style={{ overflowX: "auto" }}>
      <svg
        viewBox={`0 0 ${width} ${height}`}
        fill="none"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        className="w-full max-w-4xl font-mono"
        role="img"
        aria-labelledby={titleId}
        aria-describedby={descId}
        preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"
        style={{ width: "100%", height: "auto", maxWidth: "100%" }}
      >
        <title id={titleId}>{title}</title>
        <desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>
        <defs>
          <pattern
            id={gridId}
            width="20"
            height="20"
            patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse"
          >
            <path
              d="M 20 0 L 0 0 0 20"
              fill="none"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="0.5"
              strokeOpacity="0.03"
            />
          </pattern>
        </defs>
        <rect
          width={width}
          height={height}
          fill={`url(#${gridId})`}
          rx="6"
        />
        {children}
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}
````

### 2. DiagramCanvas.tsx — Use tokens for grid, canvas radius, arrowhead

src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx
````
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramCanvasProps = {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  className?: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
};

export function DiagramCanvas({
  children,
  width = 760,
  height = 240,
  className = "",
  title,
  description,
}: DiagramCanvasProps) {
  const titleId = `diagram-title-${React.useId()}`;
  const descId = `diagram-desc-${React.useId()}`;
  const gridId = `grid-${React.useId()}`;

  return (
    <div className={`w-full flex justify-center py-4 ${className}`} style={{ overflowX: "auto" }}>
      <svg
        viewBox={`0 0 ${width} ${height}`}
        fill="none"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        className="w-full max-w-4xl font-mono"
        role="img"
        aria-labelledby={titleId}
        aria-describedby={descId}
        preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"
        style={{ width: "100%", height: "auto", maxWidth: "100%" }}
      >
        <title id={titleId}>{title}</title>
        <desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>
        <defs>
          <pattern
            id={gridId}
            width="var(--diagram-grid-pattern-size)"
            height="var(--diagram-grid-pattern-size)"
            patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse"
          >
            <path
              d="M 20 0 L 0 0 0 20"
              fill="none"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="var(--diagram-grid-stroke-width)"
              strokeOpacity="var(--diagram-grid-stroke-opacity)"
            />
          </pattern>
          <marker
            id="arrowhead"
            markerWidth="10"
            markerHeight="7"
            refX="0"
            refY="3.5"
            orient="auto"
          >
            <polygon points="0 0, 10 3.5, 0 7" fill="var(--diagram-accent)" />
          </marker>
        </defs>
        <rect
          width={width}
          height={height}
          fill={`url(#${gridId})`}
          rx="var(--diagram-canvas-radius)"
        />
        {children}
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}
````

### 3. DiagramNode.tsx — Use tokens for all visual constants

src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx
````
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramNodeProps = {
  x: number;
  y: number;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  label: string;
  detail: string;
  active?: boolean;
  detailActive?: boolean;
  children?: React.ReactNode;
};

export function DiagramNode({
  x,
  y,
  width = 140,
  height = 60,
  label,
  detail,
  active = false,
  detailActive = false,
  children,
}: DiagramNodeProps) {
  const isCompact = height === 50;
  const labelY = isCompact ? 20 : 24;
  const detailY = isCompact ? 36 : 42;

  return (
    <g transform={`translate(${x}, ${y})`}>
      <rect
        x="0"
        y="0"
        width={width}
        height={height}
        rx="var(--diagram-node-radius)"
        stroke={active ? "var(--diagram-accent)" : "currentColor"}
        strokeWidth="var(--diagram-stroke-width)"
        strokeOpacity={active ? "var(--diagram-stroke-opacity-active)" : "var(--diagram-stroke-opacity)"}
        fill="var(--diagram-node-fill)"
      />
      <text
        x="15"
        y={labelY}
        fill={active ? "var(--diagram-text-label-fill-active)" : "var(--diagram-text-label-fill)"}
        fontSize="var(--diagram-text-label-size)"
        fontWeight="var(--diagram-text-label-weight)"
        fontFamily="var(--font-mono)"
      >
        {label}
      </text>
      <text
        x="15"
        y={detailY}
        fill={detailActive ? "var(--diagram-text-detail-fill-active)" : active ? "var(--diagram-text-detail-fill-active)" : "var(--diagram-text-detail-fill)"}
        fontSize="var(--diagram-text-detail-size)"
        fontWeight={detailActive ? "var(--diagram-text-detail-weight-active)" : "var(--diagram-text-detail-weight)"}
        fontFamily="var(--font-mono)"
      >
        {detail}
      </text>
      {children}
    </g>
  );
}
````

### 4. DiagramConnection.tsx — Use tokens for stroke widths, opacity, dasharray

src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx
````
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramConnectionProps = {
  x1: number;
  y1: number;
  x2: number;
  y2: number;
  active?: boolean;
  curved?: boolean;
  controlPoint?: { x: number; y: number };
  marker?: boolean;
};

export function DiagramConnection({
  x1,
  y1,
  x2,
  y2,
  active = false,
  curved = false,
  controlPoint,
  marker = false,
}: DiagramConnectionProps) {
  const stroke = active ? "var(--diagram-accent)" : "currentColor";
  const strokeWidth = active ? "var(--diagram-stroke-width-active)" : "var(--diagram-stroke-width)";
  const strokeOpacity = active ? "var(--diagram-connection-stroke-opacity-active)" : "var(--diagram-connection-stroke-opacity)";
  const strokeDasharray = active ? "none" : "var(--diagram-connection-stroke-dasharray)";

  if (curved && controlPoint) {
    return (
      <path
        d={`M ${x1} ${y1} Q ${controlPoint.x} ${controlPoint.y} ${x2} ${y2}`}
        stroke={stroke}
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
        strokeOpacity={strokeOpacity}
        strokeDasharray={strokeDasharray}
        fill="none"
        markerEnd={marker ? "url(#arrowhead)" : undefined}
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <line
      x1={x1}
      y1={y1}
      x2={x2}
      y2={y2}
      stroke={stroke}
      strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
      strokeOpacity={strokeOpacity}
      strokeDasharray={strokeDasharray}
      markerEnd={marker ? "url(#arrowhead)" : undefined}
    />
  );
}
````

### 5. DiagramGrid.tsx — Use tokens for grid pattern, border, corners

````
import * as React from "react";

type DiagramGridProps = {
  width: number;
  height: number;

};

export function DiagramGrid({ width, height, patternId }: DiagramGridProps) {
  return (
    <>
      <rect width={width} height={height} fill={`url(#${patternId})`} rx="var(--diagram-canvas-radius)" />
      <rect
        x="0.5"
        y="0.5"
        width={width - 1}
        height={height - 1}
        rx="var(--diagram-canvas-radius)"
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="var(--diagram-border-stroke-width)"
        strokeOpacity="var(--diagram-border-stroke-opacity)"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d="M 10 0.5 L 0.5 0.5 L 0.5 10"
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="var(--diagram-border-stroke-width)"
        strokeOpacity="var(--diagram-corner-stroke-opacity)"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${width - 10} 0.5 L ${width - 0.5} 0.5 L ${width - 0.5} 10`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="var(--diagram-border-stroke-width)"
        strokeOpacity="var(--diagram-corner-stroke-opacity)"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M 0.5 ${height - 10} L 0.5 ${height - 0.5} L 10 ${height - 0.5}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="var(--diagram-border-stroke-width)"
        strokeOpacity="var(--diagram-corner-stroke-opacity)"
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${width - 10} ${height - 0.5} L ${width - 0.5} ${height - 0.5} L ${width - 0.5} ${height - 10}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth="var(--diagram-border-stroke-width)"
        strokeOpacity="var(--diagram-corner-stroke-opacity)"
        fill="none"
      />
    </>
  );
}
````

````
      {text}

  );
````

```css
@import "tailwindcss";
@import "shadcn/tailwind.css";
```

```css
@custom-variant dark (&:where(.dark, .dark *));
```

````
@theme inline {
````

<thinking-content-7bbeb8e1441453ad999a0bbba8a46d4b>

The user is asking me to fix an error in the globals.css file. The error is on line 4 with the `@custom-variant dark (.dark &);` syntax. This is a Tailwind v4 syntax issue.

In Tailwind v4, the correct syntax for custom variants is different. The `@custom-variant` directive should use the proper syntax. Let me check what the correct syntax should be.

In Tailwind v4, the dark mode variant is typically handled differently. The `@custom-variant` directive syntax is:
```css
@custom-variant dark (&:where(.dark, .dark *));
```

Or more commonly, you'd use:
```css
@custom-variant dark (&:is(.dark *));
```

But actually, looking at the Tailwind v4 documentation, the correct way to define a dark variant that works with a class on a parent element is:

```css
@custom-variant dark (&:where(.dark, .dark *));
```

Wait, the original error was with `(&:where(.dark, .dark *))` which I changed to `(.dark &)` but that's also not quite right for Tailwind v4.

Let me think about this more carefully. In Tailwind v4, the `@custom-variant` directive allows you to define custom variants. The syntax is:

```css
@custom-variant <name> <selector>;
```

For dark mode with a class strategy (where `.dark` is on a parent element), the selector should match elements that are descendants of `.dark`. The correct selector would be:

```css
@custom-variant dark (&:is(.dark *));
```

Or using `:where` for zero specificity:
```css
@custom-variant dark (&:where(.dark *));
```

But wait, the original code had `(&:where(.dark, .dark *))` which includes both `.dark` itself and its descendants. That might be what's needed.

Actually, looking at the Tailwind v4 docs more carefully, the correct syntax for a class-based dark mode that applies to both the element with `.dark` and its children is:

```css
@custom-variant dark (&:where(.dark, .dark *));
```

But the error says there's an issue with line 4. Let me check what the actual error might be. The user showed:
```
@custom-variant dark (.dark &);
```

This syntax `(.dark &)` is not valid for `@custom-variant` in Tailwind v4. The `&` represents the current selector, so `(.dark &)` would mean `.dark .current-selector` which is backwards.

The correct syntax should be `(&:is(.dark *))` or `(&:where(.dark *))` to select the current element when it's inside a `.dark` ancestor.

But wait, the original code I had before was:
```css
@custom-variant dark (&:where(.dark, .dark *));
```

And that was working. Then I changed it to `(.dark &)` which is wrong.

Let me fix it to the correct Tailwind v4 syntax. The proper way to define a dark variant that works with a parent `.dark` class is:

```css
@custom-variant dark (&:where(.dark, .dark *));
```

This means: the current element (`&`) when it's either `.dark` itself or a descendant of `.dark` (`:where(.dark, .dark *)`).

Let me update the file with the correct syntax.

| Value | Files | Usage |
|-------|-------|-------|
| `1.2` | DiagramConnection | Active connection stroke width |
| `1` | DiagramConnection, DiagramGrid, DiagramNode | Default connection stroke, grid stroke, node border |

### 3. Border Radius

|-------|-------|-------|
| `3` | DiagramNode | Node border radius (BORDER_RADIUS constant) |

### 4. Spacing/Dimensions

| `140` | DiagramNode, architecture-diagrams, system-diagram | Default node width (NODE_WIDTH) |
| `60` | DiagramNode, architecture-diagrams, system-diagram | Default node height (NODE_HEIGHT) |
| `50` | DiagramNode, architecture-diagrams | Compact node height (NODE_HEIGHT_COMPACT) |
| `15` | DiagramNode | Label x-offset |
| `24` / `20` | DiagramNode | Label y-position (normal/compact) |
| `42` / `36` | DiagramNode | Detail y-position (normal/compact) |
| `11` | DiagramNode | Label font size |
| `9.5` | DiagramNode, DiagramCaption | Detail font size, caption font size |
| `2.5` | DiagramMarker | Default marker radius |
| `20` | DiagramCanvas, DiagramGrid | Grid pattern size |
| `0.5` | DiagramGrid | Grid line offset |
| `10` | DiagramGrid | Corner accent length |

### 5. Opacity Values
| Value | Files | Usage |
|-------|-------|-------|
| `1` | DiagramConnection | Active stroke opacity |
| `0.1` | DiagramConnection | Inactive stroke opacity |
| `0.4` | DiagramNode | Active border opacity |
| `0.18` | DiagramNode | Inactive border opacity |
| `0.03` | DiagramCanvas | Grid pattern opacity |
| `0.08` | DiagramGrid | Grid border opacity |
| `0.25` | DiagramGrid | Corner accent opacity |

### 6. Other
| Value | Files | Usage |
|-------|-------|-------|
| `3 3` | DiagramConnection | Inactive stroke dasharray |
| `none` | DiagramConnection | Active stroke dasharray |
| `10` / `7` / `3.5` | ArrowheadDef | Arrowhead dimensions |
| `9.5` | DiagramCaption | Font size |

---

## Categorization for Design Tokens

### Should Become Design Tokens (Shared Across Components)
1. **Colors** - Primary palette: `lime` (#D9F99D), `foreground` (#f3f4f6), `muted` (#9ca3af), `muted-active` (#d1d5db), `background` (#0f0f11)
2. **Stroke Widths** - `stroke.thin` (0.5), `stroke.default` (1), `stroke.thick` (1.2), `stroke.legacy` (2)
3. **Border Radius** - `radius.sm` (3), `radius.md` (6), `radius.legacy` (8)
4. **Spacing/Dimensions** - `node.width` (140), `node.height` (60), `node.heightCompact` (50), `node.labelOffset` (15), `node.labelY` (24/20), `node.detailY` (42/36), `font.size.label` (11), `font.size.detail` (9.5), `marker.radius` (2.5), `grid.size` (20), `grid.offset` (0.5), `grid.accentLength` (10)
5. **Opacity** - `opacity.active` (1), `opacity.inactive` (0.1), `opacity.borderActive` (0.4), `opacity.borderInactive` (0.18), `opacity.gridPattern` (0.03), `opacity.gridBorder` (0.08), `opacity.gridAccent` (0.25)
6. **Dash Patterns** - `dash.active` (none), `dash.inactive` (3 3)
7. **Arrowhead** - `arrowhead.width` (10), `arrowhead.height` (7), `arrowhead.refY` (3.5)

### Should NOT Become Tokens (Diagram-Specific Layout)
- Node positions (x, y coordinates in architecture-diagrams.tsx, system-diagram.tsx)
- Connection coordinates
- Canvas width/height per diagram
- Node spacing values specific to each diagram

---

### Modified: `src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx`
src/components/diagram/DiagramConnection.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";
import { diagramTokens } from "./tokens";

type DiagramConnectionProps = {
  x1: number;
  y1: number;
  x2: number;
  y2: number;
  active?: boolean;
  curved?: boolean;
  controlPoint?: { x: number; y: number };
  marker?: boolean;
};

export function DiagramConnection({
  x1,
  y1,
  x2,
  y2,
  active = false,
  curved = false,
  controlPoint,
  marker = false,
}: DiagramConnectionProps) {
  const stroke = active ? diagramTokens.colors.lime : diagramTokens.colors.currentColor;
  const strokeWidth = active ? diagramTokens.strokeWidth.thick : diagramTokens.strokeWidth.default;
  const strokeOpacity = active ? diagramTokens.opacity.active : diagramTokens.opacity.inactive;
  const strokeDasharray = active ? diagramTokens.dash.active : diagramTokens.dash.inactive;

  if (curved && controlPoint) {
    return (
      <path
        d={`M ${x1} ${y1} Q ${controlPoint.x} ${controlPoint.y} ${x2} ${y2}`}
        stroke={stroke}
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
        strokeOpacity={strokeOpacity}
        strokeDasharray={strokeDasharray}
        fill="none"
        markerEnd={marker ? "url(#arrowhead)" : undefined}
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <line
      x1={x1}
      y1={y1}
      x2={x2}
      y2={y2}
      stroke={stroke}
      strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
      strokeOpacity={strokeOpacity}
      strokeDasharray={strokeDasharray}
      markerEnd={marker ? "url(#arrowhead)" : undefined}
    />
  );
}
```

### Modified: `src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx`
src/components/diagram/DiagramCanvas.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";
import { diagramTokens } from "./tokens";

type DiagramCanvasProps = {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  className?: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
};

export function DiagramCanvas({
  children,
  width = 760,
  height = 240,
  className = "",
  title,
  description,
}: DiagramCanvasProps) {
  const titleId = `diagram-title-${React.useId()}`;
  const descId = `diagram-desc-${React.useId()}`;
  const gridId = `grid-${React.useId()}`;

  return (
    <div className={`w-full flex justify-center py-4 ${className}`} style={{ overflowX: "auto" }}>
      <svg
        viewBox={`0 0 ${width} ${height}`}
        fill="none"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
        className="w-full max-w-4xl font-mono"
        role="img"
        aria-labelledby={titleId}
        aria-describedby={descId}
        preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid meet"
        style={{ width: "100%", height: "auto", maxWidth: "100%" }}
      >
        <title id={titleId}>{title}</title>
        <desc id={descId}>{description}</desc>
        <defs>
          <pattern
            id={gridId}
            width={diagramTokens.grid.size}
            height={diagramTokens.grid.size}
            patternUnits="userSpaceOnUse"
          >
            <path
              d={`M ${diagramTokens.grid.size} 0 L 0 0 0 ${diagramTokens.grid.size}`}
              fill="none"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth={diagramTokens.strokeWidth.thin}
              strokeOpacity={diagramTokens.opacity.gridPattern}
            />
          </pattern>
        </defs>
        <rect
          width={width}
          height={height}
          fill={`url(#${gridId})`}
          rx={diagramTokens.borderRadius.md}
        />
        {children}
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}
```

### Modified: `src/components/diagram/DiagramGrid.tsx`
src/components/diagram/DiagramGrid.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";
import { diagramTokens } from "./tokens";

type DiagramGridProps = {
  width: number;
  height: number;
  patternId: string;
};

export function DiagramGrid({ width, height, patternId }: DiagramGridProps) {
  const { grid, borderRadius, strokeWidth, opacity } = diagramTokens;

  return (
    <>
      <rect width={width} height={height} fill={`url(#${patternId})`} rx={borderRadius.md} />
      <rect
        x={grid.offset}
        y={grid.offset}
        width={width - 1}
        height={height - 1}
        rx={borderRadius.md}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth.default}
        strokeOpacity={opacity.gridBorder}
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${grid.accentLength} ${grid.offset} L ${grid.offset} ${grid.offset} L ${grid.offset} ${grid.accentLength}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth.default}
        strokeOpacity={opacity.gridAccent}
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${width - grid.accentLength} ${grid.offset} L ${width - grid.offset} ${grid.offset} L ${width - grid.offset} ${grid.accentLength}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth.default}
        strokeOpacity={opacity.gridAccent}
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${grid.offset} ${height - grid.accentLength} L ${grid.offset} ${height - grid.offset} L ${grid.accentLength} ${height - grid.offset}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth.default}
        strokeOpacity={opacity.gridAccent}
        fill="none"
      />
      <path
        d={`M ${width - grid.accentLength} ${height - grid.offset} L ${width - grid.offset} ${height - grid.offset} L ${width - grid.offset} ${height - grid.accentLength}`}
        stroke="currentColor"
        strokeWidth={strokeWidth.default}
        strokeOpacity={opacity.gridAccent}
        fill="none"
      />
    </>
  );
}
```

```
import * as React from "react";
import { diagramTokens } from "./tokens";

export function ArrowheadDef() {
  const { arrowhead, colors } = diagramTokens;
  return (
    <defs>
      <marker
        id="arrowhead"
        markerWidth={arrowhead.width}
        markerHeight={arrowhead.height}
        refX={arrowhead.refX}
        refY={arrowhead.refY}
        orient="auto"
      >

      </marker>

  );
}
```

### Modified: `src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx`
src/components/diagram/DiagramNode.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";
import { diagramTokens } from "./tokens";

type DiagramNodeProps = {
  x: number;
  y: number;
  width?: number;
  height?: number;
  label: string;
  detail: string;
  active?: boolean;
  detailActive?: boolean;
  children?: React.ReactNode;
};

const {
  node: { width: NODE_WIDTH, height: NODE_HEIGHT, heightCompact: NODE_HEIGHT_COMPACT, labelOffsetX, labelY, labelYCompact, detailY, detailYCompact },
  borderRadius: { sm: BORDER_RADIUS },
  strokeWidth: { default: STROKE_WIDTH },
  colors,
  font,
  opacity,
} = diagramTokens;

export function DiagramNode({
  x,
  y,
  width = NODE_WIDTH,
  height = NODE_HEIGHT,
  label,
  detail,
  active = false,
  detailActive = false,
  children,
}: DiagramNodeProps) {
  const isCompact = height === NODE_HEIGHT_COMPACT;

  return (
    <g transform={`translate(${x}, ${y})`}>
      <rect
        x="0"
        y="0"
        width={width}
        height={height}
        rx={BORDER_RADIUS}
        stroke={active ? colors.lime : colors.currentColor}
        strokeWidth={STROKE_WIDTH}
        strokeOpacity={active ? opacity.borderActive : opacity.borderInactive}
        fill={colors.background}
      />
      <text
        x={labelOffsetX}
        y={isCompact ? labelYCompact : labelY}
        fill={active ? colors.lime : colors.foreground}
        fontSize={font.labelSize}
        fontWeight={font.labelWeight}
      >
        {label}
      </text>
      <text
        x={labelOffsetX}
        y={isCompact ? detailYCompact : detailY}
        fill={detailActive ? colors.mutedActive : active ? colors.mutedActive : colors.muted}
        fontSize={font.detailSize}
        fontWeight={detailActive ? font.detailWeightActive : font.detailWeight}
      >
        {detail}
      </text>
      {children}
    </g>
  );
}
```

```
import * as React from "react";
import {
  DiagramCanvas,
  DiagramGrid,
  DiagramNode,
  DiagramConnection,
  DiagramMarker,
  DiagramCaption,
  ArrowheadDef,
} from "@/components/diagram";
import { diagramTokens } from "@/components/diagram/tokens";

// 1. Overall System Topology
export function OverallSystemDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 220;
  const patternId = "grid-system-overall";
  const nodeY = 80;
  const connectionY = 110;
  const { node, node: { width: nodeWidth, height: nodeHeight } } = diagramTokens;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Overall System Topology"
      description="Three-node system architecture: Website Portal entry point, Scheduler Core control plane, and Node Network execution plane. Connections show data flow from website to scheduler to compute nodes."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Website */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[WEBSITE_PORTAL]"
        detail="Entry & Onboard"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Control Plane"
      >
        <DiagramMarker cx={125} cy={15} />
      </DiagramNode>

      {/* Node 3: Contributed Nodes */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[NODE_NETWORK]"
        detail="Execution Plane"
      />

      {/* Connections */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth - 45} cy={connectionY} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 2. Request Flow
export function RequestFlowDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 240;
  const patternId = "grid-flow-request";
  const nodeY = 90;
  const connectionY = 120;
  const { node: { width: nodeWidth } } = diagramTokens;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Request Flow"
      description="Request lifecycle from client submission through scheduler routing to node execution. Active path highlighted showing successful routing to EU-West node with direct result return path."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Client */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[CLIENT_INTERFACE]"
        detail="Status: SUBMITTING"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Status: ROUTING"
      />

      {/* Node 3: Selected Compute Node */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[NODE_EU_WEST]"
        detail="Status: EXECUTING"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Active Connection Paths */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      {/* Signal indicators on the active loop */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeWidth + 45} cy={connectionY} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 - 45} cy={connectionY} />

      {/* Direct Output Return Path (Subtle feedback loop at bottom) */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 + nodeWidth - 30}
        y1={connectionY + 30}
        x2={startX + 30}
        y2={connectionY + 30}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: width / 2, y: connectionY + 70 }}
      />
      <DiagramCaption
        x={width / 2}
        y={connectionY + 65}
        text="DIRECT_RESULT_PAYLOAD (verification_loop)"
      />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 3. Geographic Scheduling
export function GeographicSchedulingDiagram() {

  return (

      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Geographic Scheduling"
      description="Scheduler routing decision showing three candidate nodes with latency measurements. EU-West selected as minimum latency (12ms) vs US-East (78ms) and AP-South (284ms)."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Scheduler Node (Left Column) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={schedulerX}
        y={schedulerY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Latency Engine"
      />

      {/* Nodes (Right Column Stacked) */}
      {/* Node 1: US-East */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeightCompact}
        label="[NODE_US_EAST]"
        detail="Latency: 78ms"
      />

      {/* Node 2: EU-West (Selected) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY + nodeSpacing}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeightCompact}
        label="[NODE_EU_WEST]"
        detail="Latency: 12ms (MIN)"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Node 3: AP-South */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={nodeX}
        y={startY + nodeSpacing * 2}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeightCompact}
        label="[NODE_AP_SOUTH]"
        detail="Latency: 284ms"
      />

      {/* Routing branches */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}

        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeHeightCompact / 2}
        curved

      />

        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}

        x2={nodeX}

      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={nodeX}
        y2={startY + nodeSpacing * 2 + nodeHeightCompact / 2}
        curved
        controlPoint={{ x: 350, y: 215 }}

// 4. Distributed Inference
export function DistributedInferenceDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 280;
  const patternId = "grid-inf-distributed";
  const schedulerX = 80;
  const schedulerY = 110;
  const { node: { width: nodeWidth, height: nodeHeightCompact } } = diagramTokens;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Distributed Inference Pipeline"
      description="Model layer partitioning across three compute shards. Scheduler partitions layers 1-12 to Shard A, 13-24 to Shard B, 25-36 to Shard C. Pipeline flow shown with active connections."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Scheduler (Left) */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={schedulerX}
        y={schedulerY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Layer Partitioner"
      />

      {/* Pipeline Shards */}
      {/* Shard A */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={320}
        y={60}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeightCompact}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_A]"
        detail="Layers: 1 - 12"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Shard B */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={520}
        y={60}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeightCompact}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_B]"
        detail="Layers: 13 - 24"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Shard C */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={420}
        y={170}
        width={nodeWidth}
        height={nodeHeightCompact}
        label="[NODE_SHARD_C]"
        detail="Layers: 25 - 36"
        active
        detailActive
      />

      {/* Pipeline connection paths */}
      {/* Scheduler -> Shard A */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={schedulerX + nodeWidth}
        y1={schedulerY + 30}
        x2={320}
        y2={85}
        active
      />

      {/* Shard A -> Shard B */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={460}
        y1={85}
        x2={520}
        y2={85}
        active
      />

      {/* Shard B -> Shard C */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={590}
        y1={110}
        x2={490}
        y2={170}
        active
      />

      {/* Flow ticks along the pipeline */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={270} cy={112.5} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={490} cy={85} />
      <DiagramMarker cx={540} cy={140} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}

// 5. Future Architecture
export function PlatformStackDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 240;
  const patternId = "grid-stack-platform";
  const layerX = 120;
  const { node: { width: layerWidth, height: layerHeight } } = diagramTokens;
  const layerSpacing = 45;
  const startY = 30;

  const layers = [
    {
      label: "APPLICATION / API LAYER",
      detail: "Client SDKs, telemetry portals, developer API endpoints",
      y: startY,
      active: false,
    },
    {
      label: "ORCHESTRATION & COORDINATION LAYER",
      detail: "Geographic scheduling engine, node registries, queue models",
      y: startY + layerSpacing,
      active: true,
    },
    {
      label: "DECENTRALIZED TRANSPORT LAYER",
      detail: "P2P overlay routing, message heartbeats, secure gRPC tunnels",
      y: startY + layerSpacing * 2,
      active: false,
    },
    {
      label: "LOCAL HARDWARE EXECUTION RUNTIME",
      detail: "CUDA/ROCm device engines, local resource benchmarks, sandboxes",
      y: startY + layerSpacing * 3,
      active: false,
    },
  ];

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Future Platform Stack Architecture"
      description="Four-layer platform stack: Application API layer, Orchestration & Coordination layer (active), Decentralized Transport layer, and Local Hardware Execution Runtime layer. Each layer spans full width with descriptive details."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {layers.map((layer, index) => (
        <DiagramNode
          key={index}
          x={layerX}
          y={layer.y}
          width={layerWidth}
          height={layerHeight}
          label={layer.label}
          detail={layer.detail}
          active={layer.active}
          detailActive={layer.active}
        />
      ))}
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}
```

### Modified: `src/components/system-diagram.tsx`
src/components/system-diagram.tsx
```
import * as React from "react";
import {
  DiagramCanvas,
  DiagramGrid,
  DiagramNode,
  DiagramConnection,
  DiagramMarker,
  ArrowheadDef,
} from "@/components/diagram";
import { diagramTokens } from "@/components/diagram/tokens";

export function SystemDiagram() {
  const width = 760;
  const height = 180;
  const patternId = "grid-home-system";
  const nodeY = 60;
  const connectionY = 90;
  const { node: { width: nodeWidth, height: nodeHeight } } = diagramTokens;
  const nodeSpacing = 230;
  const startX = 80;

  return (
    <DiagramCanvas
      width={width}
      height={height}
      title="Public Intelligence System Overview"
      description="Three core components: Website Portal for onboarding, Scheduler Core as coordinator, and Compute Network for execution. Active connection from scheduler to compute network indicated by lime markers."
    >
      <DiagramGrid width={width} height={height} patternId={patternId} />
      <ArrowheadDef />

      {/* Node 1: Website */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[WEBSITE_PORTAL]"
        detail="Role: Onboarding"
      />

      {/* Node 2: Scheduler */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[SCHEDULER_CORE]"
        detail="Role: Coordinator"
      >
        <DiagramMarker cx={125} cy={15} />
      </DiagramNode>

      {/* Node 3: Global Compute Network */}
      <DiagramNode
        x={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y={nodeY}
        label="[COMPUTE_NETWORK]"
        detail="Role: Execution"
      />

      {/* CONNECTIONS (Aligned at Y=90) */}
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing}
        y2={connectionY}
      />
      <DiagramConnection
        x1={startX + nodeSpacing + nodeWidth}
        y1={connectionY}
        x2={startX + nodeSpacing * 2}
        y2={connectionY}
        active
      />

      {/* Data indicator dot */}
      <DiagramMarker cx={startX + nodeSpacing * 2 - 45} cy={connectionY} />
    </DiagramCanvas>
  );
}
```

```
import * as React from "react";
import { diagramTokens } from "@/components/diagram/tokens";

export function ArchitectureDiagram() {
  const { colors, strokeWidth, borderRadius } = diagramTokens;
  return (
    <div className="my-12 flex justify-center">
      <svg 
        width="600" 
        height="300" 
        viewBox="0 0 600 300" 
        className="w-full max-w-4xl"
        xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
      >
        {/* Website Node */}
        <rect 
          x="50" 
          y="100" 
          width="120" 
          height="80" 
          rx={borderRadius.legacy} 
          fill={colors.white} 
          stroke={colors.green} 
          strokeWidth={strokeWidth.legacy}
          className="transition-all duration-300 hover:stroke-green-500"
        />
        <text 
          x="110" 
          y="140" 
          textAnchor="middle" 
          className="fill-foreground text-sm font-medium"
        >
          Website
        </text>
        
        {/* Scheduler Node */}
        <rect 
          x="240" 
          y="100" 
          width="120" 
          height="80" 
          rx={borderRadius.legacy} 
          fill={colors.white} 
          stroke={colors.green} 
          strokeWidth={strokeWidth.legacy}
          className="transition-all duration-300 hover:stroke-green-500"
        />
        <text 
          x="300" 
          y="140" 
          textAnchor="middle" 
          className="fill-foreground text-sm font-medium"
        >
          Scheduler
        </text>
        
        {/* Global Nodes */}
        <rect 
          x="430" 
          y="60" 
          width="120" 
          height="80" 
          rx={borderRadius.legacy} 
          fill={colors.white} 
          stroke={colors.green} 
          strokeWidth={strokeWidth.legacy}
          className="transition-all duration-300 hover:stroke-green-500"
        />
        <text 
          x="490" 
          y="100" 
          textAnchor="middle" 
          className="fill-foreground text-sm font-medium"
        >
          Global Nodes
        </text>
        
        {/* Connection from Website to Scheduler */}
        <line 
          x1="170" 
          y1="140" 
          x2="240" 
          y2="140" 
          stroke={colors.green} 
          strokeWidth={strokeWidth.legacy} 
          markerEnd="url(#arrowhead)"
        />
        
        {/* Connection from Scheduler to Global Nodes */}
        <line 
          x1="360" 
          y1="140" 
          x2="430" 
          y2="100" 
          stroke={colors.green} 
          strokeWidth={strokeWidth.legacy} 
          markerEnd="url(#arrowhead)"
        />
        
        {/* Arrowhead definition */}
        <defs>
          <marker 
            id="arrowhead" 
            markerWidth="10" 
            markerHeight="7" 
            refX="0" 
            refY="3.5" 
            orient="auto"
          >
            <polygon 
              points="0 0, 10 3.5, 0 7" 
              fill={colors.green} 
            />
          </marker>
        </defs>
      </svg>
    </div>
  );
}
```

- No layout, responsiveness, typography, accessibility, or content changes

- The token system is now reusable and maintainable
